<Text>This unique Metaphysical Shop is housed in the heart of Belmont Shore.

Z Fabrique is well stocked with stick and cone incense, my main reason for shopping there, but they also resin, charcoal, carry an array of candles, crystals, ethnic art, jewelry, new age supplies, as well as esoteric goods,  and much more.

Reasonable prices per minute Card Readings are available for those who are interested and if that's your thing.

Even if you're just curious, this is a cute shop to simply browse, just make sure you venture into the back room for additional merchandise.

I don't know the woman typically at the front counter but she has always been pleasant and friendly...always willing to answer questions, eager to tell you about the shop, and provide helpful info if needed.  Don't be bashful not to strike up a conversation of the Earth's Cycles/Phases.

Other items that I shop for other than incense are The Naked Bee Sandalwood Hand Lotion, Power Mini Crystal Bracelets, and their small Tumbled Stones.

< Review>
This is a delightful little shop that is just off the beaten path. You won't find another like it in the Shore. There are so many unique items for your home and for your spirit that you could easily spend quite a while just browsing through this little place. There is an extensive and wide selection of incense that is very reasonably priced. I think it was over 15 years ago that I discovered this little gem and met the owner, Nancy Scott. She's a very warm and friendly woman who is passionate about her store and the items she carries. Do yourself a favor and get off the main street: slip down a half block (south side of 2nd, on Argonne Ave) and into Z Fabrique. I'm pretty sure you won't be disappointed!<//Review>

<Text>This is a Cantonese Restaurant known for its delicious dishes. However, the Diet Coke came in a can, no fountain, no refills. the services falls short as most of the Chinese restaurants around the Rowland Heights area. The services stop Once they placed your order on the table. They don't check back to make sure everything is good. They don't see empty glasses need refills. And surprisingly They were no thank you after I paid my bill. The interior was chic but out of place, there are disco lights hanging from the ceiling like a night club. The bathrooms were clean but the funky unfit toilet seat evidencing the careless management. So, here are my ratings:
Food 5/5 Stars
Service 2/5 Stars

Roger Goh</username>
< date>
1536096133802< /date>
<Rate>5</Rate>< text>
Been here several times. Normally i find "outside"  chinese food not appetizing because we cook well at home. However, this place has some really good dishes which i feel we would need too much effort to replicate at home. The dried scallops and egg white fried rice, the french style filet mignon, and the X.O. sauce sauteed string beans in particular are just done so perfectly, i won't even bother trying to make them at home any more... just come over here, sit down and chat away while waiting for the perfectly done dishes to be served! The bonus is the big airy space and relatively quiet (due to the big space) ambiance that allows you to speak normally instead of trying to shout to be heard. These fast food style hong kong dishes here are also much cheaper than neighboring "restaurants" which may not even taste as good. You have been warned... you could get hooked on this place.<//text>

< review>
Honestly the worst taco bell I've been to. Terrible quality control. We go in every once in a while if I dont feel like cooking dinner and there is ALWAYS something wrong with the order. The food is always lopside (meaning the ingredients are not throughout the item, such as a crunchwrap having all the meat at the bottom, lettuce tomatoes in the middle and sour cream/cheese on top?) Its to the point I dont even order a crunchwrap anymore, that's not the only item this happens with but just an example. I've gotten a simple soft taco and gotten home to realize there was no meat, only cheese and lettuce... the one thing I can say is that the workers work FAST. But once you get your meal it's literally slopped together, and all thrown into ONE bag...so everything is squashed anyway. You dont put a grilled stuff burrito on top of crunchy tacos and a gordita... it makes at least half the meal inedible. We just wont come anymore, it's not worth being disappointed and having to find something else to eat anyway. Save your time and money.<//review>

This place is not only slow, it's disgusting.

On a recent Friday night a friend wanted some quick Taco Bell. As we pulled up, the drive thru was packed. So we went inside

The reason the drive through was so busy?

The only reason I could figure is, the place smelled like a bathroom! And in not a nice way. That smell when it seems like the sewer is backing up and coming out thru the toilet.

My friend commented about it to the counter person. She just looked at us with a blank stare.

How can a food prep place smell like a backed up sewer? I've been in porta pottys that smell better.

Perhaps the selection of fast food is slim to none in rosamond. But no way would I ever go back. Not even in the drive thru. Food served in a place that filthy is disgusting.

Pass.</Text>
